### Orange Pi 5B (8GB) with Camera Module (OV13850)

#### Key Specifications:
- **Voltage Ratings**: 5V (Type-C power supply)
- **Current Ratings**: 4A (recommended power supply)
- **Power Consumption**: Not explicitly stated, but requires a 5V/4A power supply.
- **Operating Temperature Range**: Not specified in the provided text.
- **Package Type**: Development board
- **Special Features**:
  - Octa-core ARM processor (Rockchip RK3588S)
  - Supports up to 8K display output
  - Integrated AI accelerator (NPU)
  - Multiple connectivity options including HDMI, USB 3.0, USB 2.0, Gigabit Ethernet, Wi-Fi 6, and Bluetooth 5.0
  - Supports various operating systems including Android 12, Debian, and Ubuntu.
- **Moisture Sensitive Level (MSL)**: Not specified.

#### Description:
The Orange Pi 5B is a powerful single-board computer (SBC) designed for various applications, including edge computing, artificial intelligence, and smart home devices. It features a Rockchip RK3588S octa-core processor, which combines four Cortex-A76 cores and four Cortex-A55 cores, providing high performance for demanding tasks. The board supports up to 16GB of LPDDR4 RAM and offers multiple storage options, including eMMC and microSD.

#### Typical Applications:
- **High-End Tablets**: The board's processing power and graphics capabilities make it suitable for tablet applications.
- **Edge Computing**: With its AI capabilities, it can be used in edge computing scenarios for data processing and analysis.
- **Artificial Intelligence**: The built-in NPU allows for efficient AI model execution, making it ideal for AI applications.
- **Smart Home Devices**: The board can be integrated into smart home systems for automation and control.
- **Media Centers**: With support for high-resolution video output, it can serve as a media center for streaming and playback.
- **Development and Prototyping**: The extensive connectivity options and support for various operating systems make it a versatile platform for developers and hobbyists.

### Camera Module (OV13850):
The OV13850 is a 13MP MIPI camera module that can be connected to the Orange Pi 5B for high-quality image capture. It is suitable for applications requiring image processing, such as surveillance, robotics, and multimedia projects.

#### Summary:
The Orange Pi 5B with the OV13850 camera module is a robust platform for developing advanced applications in AI, multimedia, and IoT. Its powerful hardware, combined with flexible software support, makes it an excellent choice for both hobbyists and professionals looking to create innovative solutions.
